			var nApp = angular.module('nApp', ['ngCookies','novulo.kameraexpressnl','ngSanitize','novulo.cms','ngAnimate','ngTouch','ui.bootstrap']);
var regexIso8601 = /(\d{4}-[01]\d-[0-3]\dT[0-2]\d:[0-5]\d:[0-5]\d\.\d+)|(\d{4}-[01]\d-[0-3]\dT[0-2]\d:[0-5]\d:[0-5]\d)|(\d{4}-[01]\d-[0-3]\dT[0-2]\d:[0-5]\d)/;

function convertDateStringsToDates(input) {
	// Ignore things that aren't objects.
	if (typeof input !== "object") return input;

	for (var key in input) {
		if (!input.hasOwnProperty(key)) continue;

		var value = input[key];
		var match;
		// Check for string properties which look like dates.
		if (typeof value === "string" && (match = value.match(regexIso8601))) {
			var milliseconds = Date.parse(value);
			if (!isNaN(milliseconds)) {
				input[key] = new Date(milliseconds);
			}
		} else if (typeof value === "object") {
			// Recurse into object
			convertDateStringsToDates(value);
		}
	}
};

novuloCms.config(['$httpProvider', '$compileProvider', function ($httpProvider, $compileProvider) {
	//$compileProvider.debugInfoEnabled(false);
	$httpProvider.defaults.transformResponse.push(function (responseData) {
		convertDateStringsToDates(responseData);
		return responseData;
	});
}]);

			$(document).ready(function() {

    // Initialize affix and add an offset to add affix class on scroll
    //$('#mainnavbar').affix({
    //  offset: {
    //    top: 90
    //  }
    //})

    // calc offset
    var sumoffset = 0;
    $("#mainnavbar, #pagenav").each(function(index) {
        sumoffset += $(this).outerHeight()
    });

    // scrollspy
    new $.fn.scrollspy.Constructor($('body'), {
        target: '.pagenavbar',
        offset: sumoffset + 40
    });

    // sticky pagenav
    var pagenavpos = $('#pagenav').length ? $('#pagenav').offset().top : null;

    function setPagenav() {
        if (!pagenavpos) return;
        var scrollpos = $(window).scrollTop();
        $('body').toggleClass('pagenav-fixed', scrollpos + 50 > pagenavpos);
    }

    setPagenav();
    $(window).scroll(function() {
        setPagenav();
    });


    // smoothscroll
    $('a[href*=#]:not([href=#]):not(a[href=#form_email_notification]):not(a[href^=#collapse]):not(#tabs a[href^=#]):not(a[href=#myCarousel])').click(function() {
        if (location.pathname.replace(/^\//, '') == this.pathname.replace(/^\//, '') || location.hostname == this.hostname) {

            var target = $(this.hash);
            target = target.length ? target : $('[name=' + this.hash.slice(1) + ']');
            if (target.length) {
                $('html,body').animate({
                    scrollTop: target.offset().top -= sumoffset + 15
                }, 1000);
                return false;
            }
        }
    });


    // focus
    $("#fe_search_field>input").focus();

// change logo size
    // jQuery(window).scroll(function () {
    //     if (jQuery(this).scrollTop() > 40) {
    //         jQuery('#mainnavbar').addClass('scroll');
    //     } else {
    //         jQuery('#mainnavbar').removeClass('scroll');
    //     }
    // });

// pagination
$('.pagination-prev > a').attr('rel', 'prev').attr('title', 'Ga naar vorige pagina');
$('.pagination-next > a').attr('rel', 'next').attr('title', 'Ga naar volgende pagina');

});

			novuloKameraExpress.controller('dynamicMenuCtrl', ['$scope', 'lds_menuitemsService', '$filter', function ($scope, lds_menuitemsService, $filter) {
    $scope.tags = {};
    $scope.maingroup = {};
    $scope.maingroups = [];
    lds_menuitemsService.subscribe($scope, function (event, args) {
        $scope.tags = args.data.reduce(function (result, item) {
            var group = result[item['product_tag_group']] || [];
            group.push(item);
            result[item['product_tag_group']] = group;
            return result;
        }, {});
    });

    $scope.$watch('source', function (val) {
        var groups = val.reduce(function (result, item) {
            // create a node for the item, and add it to the subgroups of a parent item.
            result[item._id] = result[item._id] || { item: null, groups: [] }// may exist already as ptg.
            result[item._id].item = item;
            if (item.parent_tag_group != null) {
                result[item.parent_tag_group] = result[item.parent_tag_group] || { item: null, groups: [] }; // initialize if ptg doesn' t exist.
                result[item.parent_tag_group].groups.push(result[item._id]);
            }
            return result;
        }, []);
        // only return the root-node
        groups.forEach(function (group) {
            if (group.item != null) {
                if(group.item.product_tag_group == null) {
                    if (group.item.reference == 'product-category-ke' || group.item.reference == 'category-produits-ke') {
                        $scope.maingroup = group;
                    }
                }
            }
        });
        $scope.groups = groups;
    })

    $scope.getTags = function (sub) {
        if (typeof sub == 'undefined') { console.log("sub is undefined"); return []; }
        return $filter('filter')($scope.tags, { product_tag_group: sub._id });
    };

    $scope.$on('windowResize', function (event, currentBreakpoint, previousBreakpoint) {
        $scope.isCollapsed = (currentBreakpoint === 'xs' || currentBreakpoint === 'sm');
    });

    $scope.checkSale = function (item) {
        if (item.reference.indexOf('sale') > -1 || item.reference.indexOf('aanbieding') > -1 || item.reference.indexOf('offres') > -1) {
            return true;
        } else {
            return false;
        }
    }
}]);
